    "alldata = dict()\n",
    "for filename in files:\n",
    "    set_name = filename.split(sep='flame_')[0]\n",
    "    df_dict = pd.read_excel(filename,sheetname=None)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    df_this = pd.concat(df_dict,ignore_index=True)\n",
    "    \n",
    "    alldata[set_name] = df_this"
